# DeltaRambles C1: Separation

## Summary: The sun shines on a busy afternoon, and Mijo is once again at a precipice of a new year of darkness and light. The duality of suffering and happiness, it weaves around until it can be wrestled and used for good. ## Author's Note: A mostly prologue dealing with the plot setting up of Season 3, I guess. Further details will be added if necessary, as edits but if not, enjoy! — jmb~ --- _June 14, 2025, 14:56, Freedom Park, Cab City._ Mijo is walking on a cloudy day. "It's been.. two months, huh?" Mijo looks around him, while no one around here knows his story, and he thinks, they shouldn't anyway, it still makes him feel _alone._ "I remember that day like yesterday. The cries, the laughs and the longing once we all went our separate ways.." _Flashback._ Mijo is looking at Rhida, both in their school uniform as Rhida slowly walks away from him and the dark world opening. "I know you think higher of me, I know you all do." Mijo says to himself, as she can't hear his words from that range. "But.. I—I can't.. wrestle with these.. **separations**. They're all but one more bond broken for.." Mijo stops, as he looks at Rhida one more time before she turns to a corner, leaving him alone in his thoughts. "..good?" Mijo answers, but it's shaky, he doesn't know if it's true anymore. "It's true, I got my wish, I saw you, and... _and the Dark Pearl_ again." Mijo looks at his arms, legs and the pink notebook, that was resting nearby along with his backpack. "I just wish it didn't take so much out of me." Mijo remembered moments, many regrets, many painful fights and many defeats only barely won. "It does make for a good adventure, I guess." _Back to the Present._ He was snapped back to reality, when he absent mindedly looked at a random girl in the park that looked just a tiny bit like Rhida. "Oh, right." Mijo shrugs. "Why am I always expecting fate to be by my side?" Mijo looks at the stage in the park, which has 'JESUS' written on its background. "I can only hope that God exists in both worlds, but.." Mijo looks away. "Then again, I probably wouldn't want to meet someone that let me almost die a bunch of times, gave me powers that hurt to use, and also.." Mijo chuckles. "..these separations." Mijo continues walking. _Later, at home (June 14, 15:56)._ "Let's continue my.. walk in there." Mijo says to himself, looking at the pink notebook. Mijo stabs it with a spare pen as the dark fountain spews out. "Got the.." Mijo checks the notebooks inside his room. "Pink for Jomi's Castle World.. Blue for Dajovy.. Purple for Nuevo Leon..." Mijo nodded before stabbing the ground with *intense will* as the ground collapsed and now he was free falling. "Alright.. What's the **new enemy** this time.." Mijo thought as he landed perfectly on the lightner's platform. _No Jomi was waiting for him._ "Ah, right. I'm basically a part-time resident here. And.." Mijo scoffs. "Jomi is as busy as always." Mijo then starts walking, his full dark world form of a blue jacket and dark cyan pants. "Let's revisit something." Mijo walks to Jomi's castle as Jomi's guards meet him. "Good day, sir!" Mijo salutes them as he goes to a part of Jomi's courtyard where they put the remembrance for that version of the _Dark Pearl_ that featured **Ikari.** 'Here lies the magic-infused stone signatures of the 'Dark Pearl' as of April 11, 2025.' _Jomi - jmmcjjaa~ 'The Princess of the Dark'_ _Mijo - Mijjcaljver 'The Lightbringer'_ _Urda - Urdnmg! 'The Wind of Golden Trees'_ _Jamise - Jmsee 'The Tides Trickster'_ _JR - JJRRB 'The Bulwark Rock'_ _Lauvielle - Lvlayaa 'The Shock Lawyer.'_ _Leviente - Lvvamg 'The Flame Defender'_ _Rhida - Rhiiadrramp 'The Ice Queen'_ _Ikari - Kaiirotut 'The Lavawalker'_ Mijo goes silent as he sees the names of his friends and where they could be now. "I have... no need to _recollect_ what happened here." Mijo says. "I moved on." Mijo looks around the surrounding courtyard. "At least.. I want to believe so." Mijo sighs. "I just.. wished separations weren't so.. long and reunion so.. unstable and crazy, ugh." Mijo then salutes the Dark Pearl Statue before leaving. "I better head to the training area. Ugh, my muscles are all hurting just by crouching like this." Mijo stretches his arms. "I've gotten lazy _and_ weak." Mijo then walks as he summons his original sword and unsheathes it. "I do wish I could use this outside of here.. ugh, It'll make so much more **things** easier." Mijo sighs again, he clutches his head before saying, "Anyways, let's just.. get there." Mijo walks around, he thinks the castle looks busy.. Jomi's guards moving around, staff with documents, paper, the usual government stuff. The castle seemed so big and empty before, but that was before the **first..** and **second..** cataclysms. `"Huh, there sure are a lot of cataclysms every year or so.."` Mijo thinks to himself, he wonders if Jomi is free after the workday is done but he puts it off. Mijo goes to the training area and fiddles with the controls again. "Huh, nothing changed." Mijo mumbled, of course, he didn't really think it would but was curious to see, just in case it did. "Alright. Jomi I guess." Mijo selects Jomi Boss Battle - Medium Difficulty as the area transforms and Mijo stretches his arms and legs as he positioned himself to unleash Iaijitsu. "I—If I have to fight you then I shall." Boss Jomi says as she charges up her sword attack. "If I remember correctly, there's an easy way to defeat this version easily." Mijo eyes Boss Jomi as she unleashes sparks of electro and walls of cryo all over the arena (the training area has become an arena) as he dodges without a single slash. "Still got it.. ugh.." Mijo groans at the adrenaline coursing as well as the phantom pain. "Let's end this." Mijo touched the hilt of his blade as he unleashed many slashes and even many direct cuts to ice blocks built or thrown in Mijo's direction. "You.." Mijo dodges an ice block. "shall.." Another slash to prevent blockage. "_DIE!_" Mijo unleashes his lightning attack, going into light speed to slash around as he went back to normal speed to follow up with a pyro attack using his other sword from his time in Nuevo Leon. **"Burn!!!"** Mijo unleashes red hot flames against Boss Jomi as she disintegrates. Mijo lands as he falls to the ground on his knees being held up by the sword stabbed on the ground. "Ah—! I keep— using it. It.. keeps **hurting..** This pain.. keeps me strong!" Mijo stands up wobbly as his swords disappear. Mijo hears someone clapping behind him as he sighs and says, **"You're here."** "Great Move. Though, should've just picked the realist difficulty. Not like it would've changed a damn thing, since you're.. soo powerful. Hm, you're in the dark world again, new school year?" asked Jomi, while tilting her head to her left. Mijo sheathes his sword as he said,"Hmph, yeah." "Ah, no wonder you're training. But, things have changed since you left. Though, the city's fine. The.. other worlds are quiet. No abyssal threats since Christmas." explained Jomi, before Mijo nodded. "I see." Mijo looks around. "Things are calm for now." Mijo shrugs. "It's always like this, it feels dreadful waiting." Mijo holds Jomi's hand. "Ah! Yeah. I suppose so.. A—anyways, stop holding my hand like that, let's go to my office to chill for a bit.." said Jomi as she gently moves away Mijo's hand. "Surely, you..?" Mijo laughs a bit, finding amusement in these moments. "Of **course**. I make time." said Jomi before Mijo boops her nose, making her squeak and protect her nose using her left hand. Mijo says, "Why else would I go here?" Then he looks at the window that overlooks the area from Jomi's Office. "Though, I suppose you could've been watching me, huh?" Jomi looks down. "I—I—! Yeah. I—I could. L—Let's just move on.. already.." Jomi grabs Mijo's hand then drags him with her to her office, passing by many guards, staff and other people in the castle. "Woah, your castle's lively. I still remember when it was just.. you, me and Urda." Mijo comments as he looks at guards chatting as well as some staff too. "Oh yeah.. Haha.. How.. u—um.. time passes.." Jomi is bothered by some staff in something Mijo doesn't bother to process. `"Looks.. normal. I notice how Jomi doesn't ever pull away. It's.. comforting, but like.. weirdly.. I mean, she's me.. and I'm her... Can we hate ourselves, but love each other? Huh? Wait can that even.. well.. I do hate myself, but I like her, she's.. what I want to be.. It's just.. that's—"` Mijo's train of thought was crashed by Jomi who was now looking at him with slight concern. "Buddy. Mijo? Knight?" Jomi called out, snapping her fingers as they were in Jomi's office conveniently. "Yeah? I was just thinking about how to.. sneakily push you into be—" answered Mijo, smirking as Jomi visibly flusters and looks away, blustering. "H—Hey!" Mijo laughs before saying, "Let's.. just sit down." said Jomi as she and Mijo sat down. "Alright, I think I can infer a lot of what happened.. Just, give me the gist of your current.. 'eternal winter' situation." Mijo says as he looks outside. "O—oh.. yeah.. the.. Dajovy reclamation process has been.. slow.. at best." Jomi tugs on her purple blouse. "W—we just haven't seen much of a breakthrough in terms of that elemental robot we found, and.. admittedly, the city's tense and filled up. That's why I have a lot more people in my castle.." explained Jomi as Mijo nodded. "Ohh.. right. Your.. world is literally just your castle, and Dajovy is only like.. a city and some towns beneath?" Mijo moves his head in disappointment. "Tsk tsk.. I see. Isn't Nuevo Leon.. well.. right. That's still.. **a mess.** Hey, what has happened there anyway?" asked Mijo, as Jomi pondered while looking at the ceiling. "Um. After the *second cataclysm?* Uh.. you.. you know. It's.. been the same **desolate** stuff. We haven't like.. thought of going back there since the Cara-Rasca fight destroyed a lot of stuff.. a—and the *abyssal corruption..*" "So.. basically, you want me to go there to destroy abyssal corruption and move over some people, if I get where this is going." Mijo says. "Oh. I.. well.. I was about to say that. W—we have resonators. Sasha.. Anastasia.. But.. me and them are too important for running Dajovy to focus on Nuevo Leon. Even Sasha. Like, we can't.. umm.. well, like Nuevo Leon is hostile right? So.. there's no guarantee that we'll come back.." explained Jomi as she saddened her expression. "A—and.. as.. we've experienced.. we really can't send small-time resonators either.. risk losing them to the corruption." "I see. So it isn't all sunshine and rainbows here.. Though rainbows are rare here.. You get my point. I guess.. **I'm trading light world problems for.. dark world problems?** Where..." Mijo's a bit irritated. "Where a *single choice...* could doom an entire dark world to abyssal corruption, or I could go back, but.. I'm.. doomed if I don't pass." reflected Mijo. "S—small correction.. Don't you have to do both though..? A—at least the group ones?" asked Jomi as Mijo sardonically laughed. "Yeah. It wasn't a problem until.. it became _HALF_ of my damn school works." Mijo shakes his head. "Worse part is.. I can't... Well, I've never done it a lot with others so I don't know as much, you know? But bringing them? So I can skip stuff?" Mijo looks more exasperated. "_Problem_, I have to trust them enough so they won't become a problem lightner." Mijo asks Jomi, "You know.. uh.. yeah, Deltarune?" Jomi answers, "Yeah, it's been.. in my.. memories since the first cataclysm. Um, yeah they did release two new chapters, right?" Mijo nods and continues, "And basically, the main antagonist could be one of the lightners since a certain knight is one of them. Basically, point is, even though abyssal monsters and people are a problem, lightners could be worse as they exist in both the light and the dark." Jomi thought. "I—I guess you were lucky, huh?" Mijo nods. "Very much so." Mijo looks at the desk of Jomi, very disorganized with papers and a single lone laptop-lookalike turned off in the middle of all the regal decorations. "Anywho.. Back to the main problem. I can... *probably* solve the abyssal monster problem, but.." Mijo continues. "I might have to do it alone. And.. I also need a way to cleanse if I find a source." Jomi looks at Mijo, half worried and half disappointed. "I—I see.." Jomi sighs. "A—are you sure you're.. going alone?" Jomi reflects. "It's just.." Jomi keeps both of her hands to her chest. "It's just, I can't go with you." clarified Jomi. "I need to deal with matters here, and I'm still not sure if anyone can handle the everyday here in my position." Mijo nods understandingly as Jomi added, "I'm also not sure if anyone else can handle the abyssal corruption and cleansing..." Jomi looks down in sadness, "Sorry..." "Fine. I'm helping **you** first then." Mijo says, a bit more firm. "Is there no one that could? You really should—" Jomi interrupts him with, "H—hey! T—This is tough. alright?!" Mijo is speechless before he cleared his throat. "What I meant, is.. there's no way you **can** go? You went with us in every adventure, even during Nuevo Leon. What changed?" Mijo asks as Jomi looks down quietly, thinking before looking at Mijo, with a serious face. "It's.. a lot. Firstly, due to the growing populace.. There's some.. **discontent** in what I'm currently doing. Many many things have been said. Secondly, there's.. also a lot.. of.. **abyssal magic that doesn't come from me.** I'm guessing some people have taken matters into their own hands. Thankfully, I have some.. people that use it.. like me but.. it's.. not looking stable for me to leave for something I cannot guarantee will go smoothly. Lastly, there's been some **ongoing court war** on Scians-Chemistra or something, I have closed down a lot there, and the diplomacy..." Jomi sighs and curls up on the sofa. "I—It's a lot.. and.. I haven't thought much on how to.. truly solve all of it. As I can't go to Scians-Chemistra without leaving issues in Dajovy unsolved, but there's no.. **existential** solution. Unless it involves you lightners, or.. I guess someone as capable as me." Jomi lies down on the sofa fully as Mijo processes the situation, and also lies down on the sofa, thinking. The two are silently thinking before Mijo speaks up. "Is there a deadline?" asked Mijo, as Jomi stutters. "U—uh.. I—I don't know. But.. it's fine.. Mijo, y—you have time. I—I think? I don't want you to.. y'know." Jomi looks at Mijo looking upwards. "I don't wanna see you hurt.. again." Mijo wryly chuckled. "Hah. Being alive _is_ painful." Mijo looked at Jomi. "It's fine. I was... *naive* about destruction.**" Mijo closed his eyes, slightly **smiling. Then he opened his eyes as he looked at Jomi, still smiling. "I'm used to it. I just.." Mijo looks up before standing up and stretching his arms. "I just need more time to think, I guess, and.." Mijo stretches his neck. "Find some new lightners, I guess. Haha~" Mijo laughs sardonically. "But in all seriousness, I.. as much as I don't want to admit it, I do need companions." Mijo thinks. "So, I'll be chilling in-and-out of the dark world for some time. I still need to figure out more of the situation." Mijo looks out. "Will I be **recognizable..** Huh, yeah I am.." "Hey, Jomi? You have.. uh some clothes I could borrow for walks? My outfit is.. very recognizable, and.. I might need to change sometimes." asked Mijo, as Jomi thought. "W—we can use transformation magic..?" Mijo laughs. "Then I'll be even more recognizable. Who casually forgets the face.." Mijo moves closer to Jomi. "..of my cute, beloved oppressor?" Jomi blushes. "I—I can.. um.. still use **some** other form.. Um, I—I think, I actually haven't.. tested any.. B—because..! I didn't need to! W—without my public regal clothes and some.. hair adjustments, I'm fine..!" "Alright, so.." Mijo smirked. "You **don't have** one for me? Girl, I thought you'd have a male or androgynous disguise..." Jomi nodded flustered. "I—I.. do! I just haven't.. used them..?" Mijo laughed. "It's fine. I.. don't need it for now." Mijo turned to the door. "I'll have some more.. reflecting to do. Stay safe, Jomi, and.." Mijo looks at Jomi again, a bit apologetic. "I'm sorry for.. calling you out.. I know you know that already. Just, be cool, hmm?" Mijo pats Jomi's head as she freezes but reluctantly lets happen before Mijo leaves. "D—damn you and your.. charm..? I mean.. we're.. oh god, do _I_ have flirting skills I have no knowledge of?!" Jomi says as she looks at her office door. _June 14, 16:53, Dajovy City, Večnajazimatski District, Dajovy City Plaza_ **One of the many unspoken rules is to not disturb lightners unless you are disturbed by them, interestingly enough.** There, in the cold yet somewhat warm plaza, after a while of simply admiring the place, Mijo sits down in one of the chairs. "Let's see.." Mijo recounts whose names he can likely reach according to what fate has brought. "Urda. She's in my class this time. With the sacrifice of.. ugh, literally _everybody else."_ Mijo looks at the reader (yes, that's _you_) unintentionally, unamused before looking away. "It's as if god.. if they even exist, I am cursed with progression, I wanna stay **stagnant with my friends,** dammit." Mijo chuckled darkly. "Though.." Mijo sighs as he looks onto the people casually walking around on a fine Dajovy night, lit up with Kugol' all around, the orange hue over the white city. "We definitely had an adventure, that's for sure." Mijo looks at the massive ice-geo statue depicting an ice structure with jagged lines and straight lines being wrapped by geo rocks in Kugol'. "I guess.. ugh." Mijo is drifting off, listening to some random conversation, something about cervical spines or whatever. He's not paying attention to whether that makes sense or not. "The hospitals are.. yeah.. there's not enough... princess.. abyss.." said the words of whatever he can make out. "Damn. Right, of course." Mijo nods. "The people." Mijo thinks more. "What happens once I.. complete it though?" asked Mijo, looking up to the night sky, it's dotted with stars, though Mijo isn't sure whether they actually exist or not. "I thought it was over when Cara.. presumably died that day, or when she and Rasca were vanquished at Nuevo Leon.. Now..?" Mijo sighs. "Right, as long as something exists.." Mijo stands up. "It can be remade." Mijo summons his sword. "I should've said destroyed.. But, like.. Cara is 'I always come back' or something, so that isn't true." Mijo smirked before making his sword disappear as he started walking back to the spot to the light world. "I need to.. speak to someone, but.." Mijo stretches his arms. "It'll be a few days before then.. Let's gather as much detail." Mijo goes silent as he goes up to the light world. _Ikari and Mijo Conversation.. I actually don't know where that it's safe to talk or create one without disturbance Mijo: But if I don't have any, just meet me somewhere near the balcony, I'm usually there chilling (Urda reacted with ❤️) _June 15, 2025, 06:35, Bus Travelling Along SCTEX_ Mijo is traveling for his sister, Deciene's (shortened to Dess') boarding house for whatever college internship, he thinks. As he's riding in a bus with his parents, he's already wondering what to do with the dark world days from now. "Nuevo Leon.." Mijo murmurs as everyone else is sleeping. "I got a certain **pirate** onboard, or even the **flamewalker** if I'm lucky.. The thing is.." Mijo looks over his other contacts, and immediately closes it as he hovers over Rhida's name. Mijo goes silent for a while, before sighing. "I'm trying to move on, Rhida.. It's just.." Mijo looks at the winding roads and fields outside the bus' window. "I can't." Mijo scratches his head almost regretfully. "Who can replace you..?" "Ugh. I sound like a **fucking** idiot." Mijo scoffs. "Don't I?" Mijo looks at his mother, May right beside him, sleeping and even then, couldn't hear his mumblings. "Yeah..." Mijo continues looking onwards to the endless road ahead. "I do want to believe I'm holding out for someone, but.." Mijo sighs. "It's just not the same." Mijo shakes his head. "Never is going to be. Ugh, I keep.. remembering _her._" "I'm like those hopeless *romantics* in poems or writings.." Mijo mocks a voice. "Oh my hopeless romance..!" Mijo chuckles. "I want you to be the love of my life, the one to bear my children..!" Mijo slaps himself playfully on this, as he felt a bit embarrassed in saying this. Since first, he _just_ lost the love of life, and two, he doesn't even **want** to have children, forever. At least, that's what he keeps telling himself, even _he_ doesn't know if his **libido** is going to agree with *him* on this. "Ugh, disgusting.." Mijo keeps thinking about it anyway. "What would I even say.." Mijo thought. "Am I even.. uh.." Mijo instinctively recoils. "*Sexually attractive??"* Mijo shakes his head. "E—even so, surely we won't.. well.. I won't be dumb enough, right?!" Mijo thinks too many times where he doubted his own stupidity and was proven right. "Fuck.. I gotta start thinking about this now, right..?" Mijo thinks. "College is where my parents met and that's basically like not that far away from me now.." This train of thought has been fortunately derailed by a buzz from his phone. "Oh..?" Mijo looks, it's just a message from Dess' that is asking their ETA to the bus terminal at the big city, some place called 'Cubao'. "Makes sense.. I'll just reply." This got him about minutes of distraction from his thoughts as he switched topics, dissociating like a '**boss',** apparently. _UP Diliman, Quezon City. 10:30. Still June 15._ Mijo is consciously (or subconsciously, he can't tell sometimes) is walking behind most of the other 'college seniors' in his immediate family, like his sister Dess, Lentz (his aunt's kid, also indirectly older sis) and Ardo, her cousin's boyfriend (?). Honestly, whatever the friend group this is supposed to be Mijo can't tell, and he thinks that this is irrelevant to the dark world anyway, so.. he once again drifts off into his own thoughts while walking the pathways of this prestigious college. "I can't stop thinking about college." Mijo says to himself. "It's like.. *a looming threat* with a far-enough deadline to where I can chill a day without being harmed, but chill for too long and **destroy yourself..**" Mijo chuckles darkly. "Just like the dark world, I wonder why.." Mijo looks at the reader (*yes, he keeps looking at you..*) **again** before looking away. "Anyway, besides the point. The dark world's easier for me." "I have experience, if necessary I can definitely bring in new lightners to the dark world.." Mijo thinks. "My only problem is.." Mijo looks to the vast green fields of the university, a luxury for a public and popular one. "Well.." Mijo sighs. "_That_ life." Mijo doesn't know if the haze that suddenly crept into his mind is because of this, but, he's hazy in thinking so he can't process it well. "I.. have been waiting for _so long_ to end _that_ life." Mijo, even though he sees no one touch his shoulder, still feels something crawling on his skin. "Coming back.." Mijo narrows his eyes. "..Feels _so bad._" Mijo reflects on his summer vacation. "For how many times I crashed out.." Mijo chuckles darkly. "I don't know if I'll... _feel_ like that again." Mijo crosses the 'Tau Alpha Walkway' as he looks onto stagnant waters, even more grassy fields, and concrete bridges. "Do I feel..?" Mijo thinks. "I do though." Mijo further reflects. "It's not that I don't. In fact, it I can process it, I'll definitely have a reaction, and by definition, a feeling but.." Mijo can't shrug off something this important. "Ugh. It's.. hard to try and feel something's **worth it** if... if.." Mijo thinks to the hell that _was_ Nuevo Leon before its desolation, wars and destruction.. Constant fighting, dark or light world, he'd never stopped fighting. "_Everything else hurts._" Mijo just feels exhausted just by thinking about the months leading up to the end of that school year. He also starts to feel feelings he can't even name, something sad, something angry, something in-between.. "Fuck. I have to learn to be **better.**" Mijo tried to taste the hollow words in his mouth. "Or.. whatever that means." Mijo looks at the trees providing shade to the campus, making sure the sun doesn't fully gaze upon his soul. "If I go to the dark world with _them again_, would it be a repeat of last time?" Mijo questions this, but he knows the answer is never clear for him. "I.. I'll have to plan first. I can't let my past interfere with my future." Mijo says, but even *he* doesn't believe it, he's wondering if he will _ever_ do though. _June 15, 12:00, Manila City's Chinatown._ Mijo is walking in this hustling and bustling part of the city, where multiple stores congregate and coagulate into a lot of people buying, chatting, selling, waiting and whatever is to do in this fine part of the city. As for Mijo, he **heavily** dislikes this part of the city, not only because it's filled with many many people, but also it reminds him of Dajovy, and it's *overpopulation crisis.* As his group that includes May, Dess', and Lentz go around and stop at food places, Mijo thinks as he drifts off again. "It's.. weird thinking like I'm about to die once school rolls in." Mijo thinks back to a vague dream he had on the bus ride. "It.. featured me, being left alone _again_ by Urda and Ikari for.. _various_ reasons I can't remember, but.." Mijo gets an ice cream small cup from May. "But.. it's probably something dumb like..." Mijo starts eating the ice cream as they move again. "Outside perspective or.." Mijo looks at a person that had the same hairstyle as Urda before she disappeared. "..they moved on?" Mijo eats another scoop. "It's.. weird. I dread the day, yet it's so.." Mijo goes under a big umbrella that's held up because it was being used by a local street vendor selling dragon fruit flavored bubble tea. "...near. I guess it's because I have to do it. But, it's more than that.." The world disappears in his mind for a minute as he starts monologuing properly. "In the dark world.. I was.. **never** a **good** leader." Mijo imagines Jomi. "She is." Mijo thinks back to the cyber world. "I only was one because of my powers. Because I felt.. powerful." Mijo imagines Jomi and Cara. "She.. used to be powerless and now powerful.. Me? Have I been that?" Mijo imagines the Dark Pearl. "They'd all say.." Mijo sees the Dark Pearl cheering on and doing excellent maneuvers because of Mijo. "You're such a great leader, Mijo! But.." Mijo imagined himself looking at his school during one of many days of normalcy. "I never amounted to anything outside of it. In fact," Mijo sees the grades in his report card, from 1st to the 4th quarter, most middle of the road, others a complete failure. **"I failed."** "But.. I'm still here aren't I?" Mijo thinks to the last meeting of him and Rhida. "Just.. not the same individual. But.. the same _circumstances_ haven't changed." Mijo looks at the gate of the school. "Same problems, same authority, and the same dread." Mijo sighs as the imaginary world shatters, the Chinatown coming back to his senses. "Just another day of being me." "Hey, Mijo~" Dess says. "Try this!" Dess shoves the boba dragon fruit mix as he reluctantly does so. Then afterwards, he commented, "It tastes like dragon fruit liquid sugary mess." Dess chuckled. "Yeah.. But it's fun!" # DeltaRambles C3S3: Tired of Dreaming

## Summary: Mijo and Rhida, pyro (and electro) and cryo.. The duo of old and.. new? Across the barren lands of Nuevo Leon, and the depths of Mijo's psyche, where shall the wind take them? Mijo, as the Lightbringer, holding the light and the lone bearer of shine is now faltering as the miracle of fate returns to seal his fate, Rhida. ## Author's Note: Saita — Mijo lightning whips Niese — Rhida ice spears Flost — Mijo large sword attack 'The Lightbringer's Dawn' — Mijo's sword Lance of Сохранение (Sohranenie) — Amber Lance that controls the big robot, used as a mirage weapon for Mijo. --- _Another week has passed.. July 18._ Mijo is sat on a hillside near the castle, but also where it overlooks Dajovy City. Mijo plays the chords to 'You Know You're Right (Demo Acoustic)' as he is mumbling most of the time to memorize the chord progression. _Then.. one more time. He starts singing._ "This is in me in love again.." Mijo continues playing. "You'll never know.." Mijo looks at the castle. "Everything I've ever known.." Mijo looks to Dajovy. "Dream.." Mijo reflects on his life, the magical world and the light boring one beside it, it always seemed like a dream. A dream he hoped, he'd never awake from. "It's wrong in every point of view.." Mijo's emotions slightly make the guitar output distorted electrical sounds. "I couldn't breathe if I was you.." "She will see another me.." Mijo's tears started forming. "When I'm through melting.." Rhida leaves. --- ## Author's Note: So, let's end it off there, I.. did not expect this chapter to go this way, and I am not that happy with how I characterized Mijo, as in.. well, IDK, it just feels that he's *too tragic??* Like, it feels like 'fixing' this mess of a character in like character development, it's like he's not a perfect hero, but *HE IS ONE.* I want characters to recognize both the light he shines, as well as the mortal human self that is flawed. I am not sure if this is a good way to move this, especially since I personally feel that the 'obsession' I intentionally made Mijo somewhat hyperbolic in how he says it due to his current mental state, I feel that I haven't showed enough 'good' Mijo moments to assume he can do better, though to be fair, this is only a chapter that focuses on his problems with Rhida, not that they never had good memories. I intended to add a Dark Pearl Section, but.. I think it's better as a separate chapter, maybe focusing on another POV after three straight Mijo ones that delve deeper into his psyche. Also because of how I wrote these parts. --- ### Oh, and sidenote, after much reflection, my answer to 'Mijo is profoundly human'; I agree, in that by the focus of Mijo here, we simply set up that he shouldn't and couldn't hold the world by himself, and that his flaws shown in his interactions with Jomi and Rhida show how he isn't perfect, but not exactly ireedemable.. It's a very complicated process, and.. It's just.. when Jomi said 'it keeps happening whenever a dark world opens' she is indirectly saying that my writing revolves around Mijo and how he constantly changes and finds himself in new ground; firstly, establishes the lightbringer, then next arc, reinforces it while cracks show, then current arc, the decay. I think I feel a bit overwhelmed because it's something that requires delicate healing that I usually don't do (like, usually the heroes aren't visibly flawed in a way that feels viscerally real, i.e. Jomi's arc of from scared puppet vessel to her own princess of right feels more fantastical than ciinically depressed heavily pressured Mijo, which since he is basically us (IRL) but havign a magical world to enter, his problems are more emotionally consuming for me to write, even Rhida too! It's just that since Mijo is the Main character, he's the one most explored. I want to do other chars, but often, Mijo's character development drives the plot so yeah. --- Anyway, I think that's about it, I'll keep going, and see where the story goes. I won't change much drastically, as this was a product of it's time, and if I'm not happy with it now, I might see it differently months from now, after going through more things and writing more. See ya, my readers! Good day, peace and have a safe day ahead~! — jmb~ | 23:44 | July 31, 2025 |💜 ✨⚔️❄️ 💜

Okay, so originally a spinoff origin story involving Ascilla has become way too important for the story to be left there so now, it follows C5S3! The Blazing Sun. So, any notes? Well, took me 3 months again, so I suppose that's concerning considering the length, but I am not a full time artisté. Um, I've been.. hard at work trying to finish C5S3 btw. Yes, if you're seeing this after, yes, I completed this before that. There's just a lotta fighting, y'know? I gotta think a lot more about that! Anyway, I don't think it'll take long if everything goes smoothly. I'd want to have a connected story that can be viewed from beginning to end. But, what about the characters? Well, while I focused a lot on Ascilla this time, it''s.. been cathartic to write her. Especially with her origin story. I wanted to have a character that'd be a cool and mysterious but also playful persona. I also just like characters like Ascilla in general. Her design is.. well, if you've seen HSR Evernight and WuWa Camellya, you'd understand this is an evolution of my previous obsessions. I also tried to progress Rhida x Mijo in a meaningful way, but we'll see how my romance writing is haha because I got beat down (metaphorically) when a beta reader went through it. We'll see. Also also, Dom Pez mentioned! He's.. well, you'll see in the next chapter but there was a reason why he was picked. I wanted to do a section wide thing for a while and I think the next chapter has been the time to do so. In case you're wondering, Dom Pez is a brief character that you don't know about much because I didn't bother to, hah. But, yeah, he makes appearances in canon main, like the last chapter! Y'all, I can't wait to write the entire story arc out. Ascilla's so fun to write! "Hey, wanna fight snakes? *Rod of Asclepius: Ordí Phidión.*" JR summoned hordes of snakes to swarm Dom as he used his anemo to blow them off his feet while slashing them with his axe. "Wait.. w—why is that a sword though..?" Jomi asked JR, temporarily snapped out of her mind palace by JR's weapon. "I am using my staff to do this, however.. with the sword, I can use a tactical snake when someone gets close. He's not even near me, but I have to be prepared." Jomi nodded as she looked around her. "I know who this.. Ascilla is. She calls herself 'Lady Ascilla'.. And, as you've probably guessed, he's connected to her in some way..." Jomi is unsure whether to fully reveal Ascilla's origin. "I—It's weird she's being specific about the **Abyss Order**, because.. I know one thing from her," Jomi looks at JR. "She *loves* Mijo. You might think this is a weird way to do so, and it is. But, one thing about that is she probably won't intentionally put a target on his back unless she had other goals in her mind that override that **instinct.**" Jomi clutched her head. "Could.. there be more to this than just a 'Lightner Showdown'?" JR sighs. "Seems like we need to find Mijo as soon as possible then." JR then deflects a hit from the battle-axe of Dom. "Yeah, but now I know you're not here for that, you didn't even know **about** it! I can't **eliminate** you anyway, all I ask for is a **fair** fight!" answered Dom, as JR black eyes glowed red. "Hm? A fair fight?" JR twirled his staff as the ground around Dom shook. "I'm more **willing** than you think." JR made the ground launch Dom up as Dom looked surprised, and out-of-balance before charging towards JR with his anemo. *"Dom Ultimate: Wind Slash!!* JR countered with, "*Sword of Asclepius: Phídia, Prostatépste!*" A tornado hit a swarm of snakes, as JR dodged while Jomi was suddenly surprised by the escalation and tried to block but was hit by some of the snakes and blown a bit back by the wind. "We're **done** here." JR tried to dash to where Dom was where he almost got hit by Dom's predicted strike, then he summoned his kitchen knife to slice Dom's arm, making a large cut, but not enough to fully cut the arm as Dom was knocked down. I want *anyone else* to decide the fates of people here." JR moved to Jomi, as she was healing herself and looking aimlessly. "Come on, I know where Mijo's direction is. If that Dom is lying, there's nothing we can do, but..." JR side-eyes Dom behind him. "...he has to be there, right?" Jomi answers, "Probably, but.. I don't want to assume. Yes, he could be trying to close the fountain as fast as possible, and believes *he alone* is enough." Jomi sighs. "Though, judging by the rules..." Jomi dusts off her clothes. "Lady Ascilla.. you.. you.. don't need to know who **she** is, only that she is both the **maker and arbitrator of the 'showdown'.**" Jomi thinks, "If.. what I **think** is right, Mijo is guaranteed safe. JR and Jomi nod to each other before running. _11:10, Unknown Dark World, City Ruins, South East of City 'Center'_ "Again." Mijo slashes another abyssal monster. "And again." "Then, the *actual* **showdown** begins~" Jomi and JR enter, determined. --- ### Author's Note: Woah woah woah!!! An actual done chapter?! Only took.. 3 months! Wow, I am... unsurprised. Fellas, can I work on this chapter in like, two weeks? I dunno, because there are those rare high moments of glorious work, but also the stupor of nothingness that seeks to sap away the very meaning of your existence. I find myself at an impasse whenever I write chapters this long, mainly because I want to finish them with a great arc and coherent plot, but at the same time, I want to keep moving forward with new ideas. You'll wonder why there's new concepts such as 'nihility' in a supposedly light and dark elemental system, but you'll see why I have added more visible paths of philosophy and relate them to the power very soon. Like, next chapter, probably. I want to keep innovating on my magic system. It is sometimes unintentional, but I do try and frame when the magic system gets updated to stages in the story. Remember when techniques didn't exist in DeltaRambles? Yeah, I just sorta retroactively added them. I like them, they help me expand on character without burdening you on why too much. Also, I will explain why there is a huge timeskip and why Laire, Cassie and Ayena are the focused characters instead of the implied other 10 in a later commentary / spinoff chapter. I figured that a story already focused on Mijo should focus on Mijo, and finish his arc first before expanding on what happened outside of him. While he isn't the center of the universe, being *that* strong tends to attract the worst type of people. Anyways, I don't got much to say, I ideally want to finish this arc as soon as possible, so I'll hold off on saying too much about my thoughts on my own writing. Ideally in the other author's note following this chapter, or the author's commentary for this month. Thank you for reading, good day, good bye, and peace~! — jmb~ | May 09, 2026 | 00:50 | 🌹🏟️⬛☀️ | ---

# DeltaRambles C8S3: The Blazing Sun, Destined to Rise

## Summary: The Lightbringer opens his eyes in an endless cycle of pain. The chained breaks free and the sun almost burns all, yet not all hope has been lost. The dark world *will be closed,* and everything should turn to normal. But normality isn't what Mijo truly feels as he oscillates between numbness and anger, breaking hearts along the way. The Blazing Sun has two paths, lighting up the dawn or burning it all away in destruction's wildfire. ### timeline: jmb | May 09, 2026 | 03:09 - 03:44, 14:00 - 17:09 | Den' Pobedy! | jmb | May 19, 2026 | 18:49 - 20:10 | 3, 2, 1... Killshot! | jmb | May 20, 2026 | 23:48 - 03:15, 3:47 - 4:39 | ao3 writer curse is real lol /s | jmb | May 21, 2026 | 23:35 - 04:37 | fnaf 2 / flash cw | jmb | May 22, 2026 | 16:30 - 17:38 | bato | jmb | May 26, 2026 | 16:02 - 17:19, 22:29 - 02:04 | jlnne | ### Author's Note: I had a hard time deciding the plot, themes and scenes of this chapter. The aftermath, and this arc, required more words than I thought possible. Hopefully you still enjoy it, even with the choices I have made. — jmb~ --- _Unknown Place, Unknown Time._ Mijo opens his eyes, as his body was still burning in his *divine form.* "What... happened?" Mijo looks around, only a single island of sand, with a single massive sakura tree was visible. There are thousands of unknown equipment from battle swords, guns, masks and magical staffs floating on what seems to be water surrounding the island. Mijo finds his sword beside him and picks it up as monsters roar and start approaching the tree and him. "What..." Mijo starts floating as the monsters approach the tree, some throw projectiles that when they hit the tree, Mijo felt something burn inside him, agony and rage mixing into flame luminously burning his body. "I remember..." Mijo points his blade to the abyss monsters going through the weapons to get the tree. "I can't let them pass at any cost." Mijo looks at the tree. "I don't know if it'll be destroyed but..." then looks at the monsters making it to the sandy shore. "...seeing these *destructive creations* of the abyss fills me with **rage.**" The monsters start approaching the tree just as Mijo was descending upon the ground. "I have nothing to say other than..." ***"Die."*** Mijo landed near the tree, sending monsters back as he fought each and every monster. They swarmed him but his blazing body torched the monsters while he cut through them like butter. His flame burned as he moved around the tree, agony increasing yet he remained constantly focused in battle. When his sword was focused on another enemy, and his left hand was free, he punched through enemies. It teared through hard and soft flesh and bone, so it hurt to do this, however, he was already running on the constant agony flowing through his entire body. He continued this, going beyond the vicinity of the tree and slashing through monsters. It seemed that the *real goal* was him, as they had stopped attacking the tree altogether, the equipment remained unused by the monsters, instead being caught in the crossfire and burnt away by Mijo's pyro. His electro was nonexistent in this form, instead resonating with the deep anger that fuels destruction. Mijo groans as, without enemies to burn, the pain that wasn't fully comprehended, consumed his very being. "Can't... sit still. Must.. burn." Mijo looks down, at the sand, then the water and sighs. Mijo looks at the area, able to fully appreciate it now that he's alone. However, he finds that he's stuck in some place where the dark blue sky and horizon seem to stretch endlessly. Mijo appreciates the view, even if there is no sun above, the only thing illuminating the place being the tree and himself. Then he hears a monster's roar. He stands up, as he looks around him to see monsters rising and approaching his position. "I.. I don't know when I'll be given the time to escape but..." Mijo looks at the tree. "It seems that tree has been tied to my well-being, for worse." Mijo stands up as he felt the flames in his body, his very blood at this moment like flowing lava. "So, I will burn." Mijo prepares to attack. "**Burn** until I have *my tomorrow.*" **Mijo screams out as he attacks the monsters all around him.** **Wave 2** Mijo keeps moving forward. **Wave 4** Mijo doesn't stop. **Wave 16** Mijo feels his flame flickering, he decides to sustain his form by taking a branch of the tree and embedding it in his burning chest. This kept the flame going, as he saw the tree quickly regrew the branch, then when he burnt more to keep his fight going, he saw the branch disappear and integrate itself within his body, causing some of his body's scars to regrow, but still be marred by golden flame. **Wave 32** Mijo will never stop moving forward. **Wave 64** Mijo saw that the 'water' actually makes great fuel for the flames, and so used it to destroy hundreds of monsters all at once. **Wave 128** Mijo noticed his hair was flame-resistant, but his top clothes have all but burnt. He shrugged and looked at the view from the front of Vesalius' Classroom, where people are walking around, some setting up for tonight. "Even if I'm not included, who cares?" Mijo asks to himself, before looking at Urda. "I used to.. care about dancing with someone, or dressing up for someone." he continued before chuckling a bit manically. "Now I'm just here to laugh at the dance, the speeches and the music." Mijo brushes his hair softly. "That's fun.." Mijo sighs and looks side-to-side. "...probably." Urda is a bit surprised by his monologue and nods quietly, "Right... I.. um.. I'm going." She turns around before turning back to look at Mijo, a bit uneasy but determined. "Uh, you.. said you'd... um, accompany me so.. I'll wait for you, okay?" reminded Urda as Mijo adjusted his glasses. "Yeah, yeah." he says, a bit annoyed. "I know, I.. I'll do that, heh." he added, before Urda narrowed her eyes, sighed and waved goodbye with a smile before walking away. "Hah.. I feel weird." said Mijo, as he manually blinked his eyes to reset his vision. "Looks like the room's cleaned up. I should go." he comments, as he goes pick his stuff up near the door. "I should... talk to Ascilla, I think." he mumbled, as he carried his sling bag and walked across the SB Building's second floor hallway. He was heading to the right stariwell as he thought about it. "My sis hasn't arrived to pick me up yet so I should take the time to talk to Ascilla..." Mijo walks down the stairs. "Could I just call her?" he thinks, as he snickered at the thought. "Someone at *my* beck and call..." Mijo smiles, he feels *elated* about it for some reason, but he quickly goes back to a relaxed face as he walks to the front of the SB Building where some chairs and tables are at. Mijo puts his bag down before saying, "Hmm.. okay, I think I know what to do." Mijo smiled before calling, **"Appear, my dear Ascilla~"** as he saw a red mist form and Ascilla appearing. The red mist dissipates as Ascilla fell to the ground, with an "Oof!" Mijo tilted his head in confusion as Ascilla opened her eyes and tried to stand up, with her left arm while wincing when the cloth on her right arm touched the healing burns. "Where am I..?" asked Ascilla, before she noticed Mijo and realized where she was. "The.. light world? Oh, you must've figured out that I can be called." Ascilla sighs. "I didn't want you to know, it'd be inconvenient." Ascilla waves with her left hand to greet Mijo. "Hello? Why did you call me?" asked Ascilla, as Mijo looked at her before noticing her burnt hand as Ascilla hid it when she realized he was looking at it. "Aw don't look at that! I'm.. mostly fine." exclaimed Ascilla, as she smiled. "Why didn't you tell me everything about the game?" asked Mijo, as his eyelids slightly closed. "I.. now, that's.. a first hard question," Ascilla looked to be in thought, before answering with a soft fond voice. "If I told you everything, you would.. try to close the fountain." she answered, before looking uneasy. "Then, the Abyss Order would've went to Nuevo Leon instead." she continued, as Mijo laughed and replied, "So? Send us there then." Ascilla gasps, "And cause unnecessary damage? No way!" Ascilla giggled, "I found an excellent dark world, made sure it was the world where you lightners would end up, even made it enticing to Arlen, saying you'd be there—" Mijo came up to Ascilla and pulled her right hand close to him making her whimper and hiss, "Mijo—! Get off—!" Ascilla tries to push him back using her left hand but Mijo pushed that hand off, making Mijo's hold dig in. "Nngh—! Let go!" Ascilla tries moving her right hand but she's breathing unevenly, her vision was swimming with the intense pain. Ascilla faints as she disappears in a red mist while Mijo watched her do so as he realized he was talking and holding her in a public school space. When he looked around, Ikari was just looking at him all weirded out. "Eh, dude? Why were you just talking to.. uh.. someone?" asked Ikari, as Mijo shook his head. "It's.. it was just.." Mijo was speechless. "I was just... talking to myself. I.. often act weird like that, okay?" answered Mijo, as Ikari's eyebrows went up. "Wha—? O—Okay..?" replied Ikari as she looked away. "Still weird..." Mijo sighs and sat back down near his bag. "I.. might've been too harsh." murmured Mijo, as he replayed Ascilla's genuine pain, but he wondered why she didn't use magic. "Maybe she can't here, or she's recovering." Mijo felt catharsis from hurting Ascilla, but at the same time, a simmering guilt he couldn't quite feel fully yet. "She deserved it." he says calmly, before looking at his phone as his sister messaged him that she has arrived. "Yeah." he repeated before standing up and grabbing his phone and bag, then walking away. _December 18, 15:30, Jomi's Castle, Jomi's Bedroom._ "I swear it was in my bedroom..." Ascilla used her left hand to feel her chest flower's petals. "At least, on myself." Speechless?" asked Ascilla as she was watching Jomi's side profile. "Well, yeah..." replied Jomi, before looking at Ascilla's left hand. "Do you love him?" asked Jomi, as Ascilla had an audible grumble before laying down beside Jomi. "I knew it potentially existed. But, I thought that Arlen would just overwhelm Mijo with his allies instead of using some... deus ex machina to do so." reflected Ascilla, as she sighed. "I thought he'd want that second confrontation to heal his pride but..." Ascilla raised her hands in defeat. "I guess trapping him inside for *240,000 years* was a better deal." Jomi gasped and asked, "M—Mijo was trapped for...?" Ascilla was silent when she realized the magnitude of that information before sighing and turning her back on Jomi to face the wall. "Yes." she says, before closing her eyes. "If you want to punish me for it, go ahead, just do it later." she added, before curling up. "Just let me die in sleep." Jomi's tears fell as she realized Arlen's whole plan with the box. "He was... no.. but.. why? Why do that? It isn't... w—what if he survives? Didn't he think of that?" she blurted out, as Ascilla didn't respond, already trying to sleep. "He.. he has to go." said Jomi, as she held Ascilla's left hand. "Cara fought for me a lot of the time, and... I can hold my own— it's just..." added Jomi, before wrapping herself around Ascilla making the flower lady gasp awake. "...he's too good at fighting. Mijo can but.. if.." continued Jomi before crying on Ascilla's back and muffling her words. Ascilla's eyes were open but she was unable to speak. She felt uncomfortable being here, but she couldn't leave Jomi behind like that. After all, she *caused it, right?* Ascilla didn't have to tell her the truth, she didn't have to even explain the box, yet she did. `"Selfish, aren't I?"`thought Ascilla as Jomi was still wrapped around her, the warmness permeating her body. `"Telling the poor princess my problems..."` she further thought, but yet she couldn't find a reason to feel guilty for it. Jomi did ask her, and she answered honestly. Ascilla then felt her chest flower quiver, as the warmness reached her heart. `"But, I invited myself in. She would have a peaceful night if it wasn't for me..."` she then paused, as Jomi sniffles slowly stopped and just Jomi's tight hold on her remained. `"Yet, she... didn't kick me out."` thought Ascilla, before turning around to make her view the ceiling while Jomi adjusted unconsciously, still holding her tightly. She then raised her right hand, still burnt, but Ascilla can observe it healing in some areas. "Without this, she probably would've kicked me out." observed Ascilla before she snorted. "But... it is what it is." added Ascilla before putting her hand down. Ascilla's eyes looked at Jomi's sleeping face, with a deep flush of red and dried up tears. "I wonder if you clocked out..." she murmured before closing her eyes. "Not my job..." she whispered before falling asleep. _December 18, 16:30, Cab City, Honrato High, Near School Gate_ Mijo walks calmly as he observes the surroundings. Especially with Mijo's character arc. The box, burning of Ascilla, the unraveling of Mijo to Urda, and just.. all of it. It's hard for me to describe what I feel about this chapter. Because, this is way out of the outline, but this also feels like the best series of scenes I probably could've created. I also would like to share something with you in the next author's note that boils down to, "Should I do a time-skip, or extend the chapters?". You'll see why. It's like making it to the end of the road of some era of your life realizing it was about as expected in the feelings side, but in a different pace and exact events as you thought it would be. "Thank you for worrying, but... *we got it.*" Sasha puts her hands behind her head. "It's not like we're **completely** oblivious to foreigners. We have you lightners, and the *beloved princess.*" Sasha looks at the ceiling just as the train stopped. "We can only *persevere,* like **you.**" Sasha stands up and takes her scythe. "Anyways, wanna come with me? You know *some*, and you'll probably meet new people! Come on, like the old times." Mijo nodded before standing up. "Yeah yeah. I was planning on talking to them anyway..." Mijo walks to the traincar's exit as he sees the more taller buildings of Pebble Town, but still modest and smaller in density than above. Mijo commented, "*I wonder where my friends are...?*" before walking with Sasha. --- _April 05, 08:30, Dark World, Jomi's Castle, Mijo & Rhida's Bedroom._ "Ah.. this feels weird on me." said Mijo, as Ascilla is helping him wear a red dress he borrowed from Jomi. "Aw, really?" asked Ascilla, as she was wearing a full red gradient black tuxedo, with the bowtie replaced by a camellia flower. She was still also wearing her camellia earrings, had black eyeshadow and long eyelashes. Her hair accessories and hair clips also remain. "It's just for a small gathering between your friends..." Ascilla shrugged. "Besides, I *heard* you **made** a temporary transformation potion for.. around twelve hours." Ascilla grinned. "Quite impressive, dear. Still not as *refined* as the princess, oh well. I suppose a late night session doesn't bode well for long-term health..." Mijo groans at the statment as he replied, "H—Hey! I.. know I haven' been sleeping early.. shut up. Getting those Linux computers, as well as potions working is.. time consuming. Luckily, there's no math... well, no, but only simple math." Ascilla chuckled. "Then no wonder you can't progress past the twenty-four hour mark.. ah well, you'll learn it in time." Mijo goes to his desk and picks up the potion, swirling the pink liquid inside the makeshift small cube vial. "I.. I'm not sure if I should do this. *Some* of my friends are going to be there, and.." Mijo faintly blushed. "**Rhida...**" Ascilla replied with a smug grin, "Relax, just say you're trying out something. Besides, these lightners all have their own schedules, friends, it's *rare* to get them all together in the dark world, in one room." Ascilla sighs. "Poor princess, I never know where she gets the energy to do this.." Mijo nods. "Alright, just this once." Mijo is unsure, but drinks it anyway. *She (Mijo)* feels her body transform, some widening there, some added weight on her chest there, and a wave of warmness following the weird sensations at her groin stopping, she was ready. "Ah, you *are ready, dear.*" commented Ascilla, smiling with her head slightly tilted to her left. "Why.. are you doing that?" asked Mijo, as Ascilla put her head back at normal tilt and turned her back towards Mijo. "A *lady's secret~*" Ascilla summons her umbrella and disappeared as Jomi knocked on the bedroom door. "Mijo...! Y—you done? We should meet them now... they're **getting** impatient." said Jomi through the door, as Mijo sighed anxiously and opened the door. "Ah.. so.. Ascilla wasn't joking, huh?" commented Jomi, as she looked at Mijo's outfit. Mijo had her white hair drape down to her chest, she had no makeup on, her red dress was simple, and her purple heels were also taken from Jomi. Mijo also took one of Jomi's clear black wrap-around glasses, and looked unamused. Mijo said, "Hello.. um, I didn't put on makeup, Ascilla complained I was **moving** too much, and my eyes couldn't stay still.." Jomi nods and replied, "I understand..? I don't put on a lot myself, a—and rarely too! Um, though Ascilla has been.. um.. nevermind. Let's save that for some other time. Let's go and meet them!" Jomi guides Mijo, still a bit unsteady at her new heels to the Dark Pearl Hangout Room. _April 05, 08:35, Dark World, Jomi's Castle, Dark Pearl Hangout Room._ **Mijo walks into the scene, as the *Dark Pearl* witnesses Mijo's new form and Jomi.** "M—Mijo..?" said Rhida, as she was amazed. "D—Didn't umm.. w—wait.. who's Mijo here?" asked Rhida, as Mijo sighed and looked at Jomi. "Ah, well.. the one in the red dress is Mijo. I'm just in my purple nightgown...! I—In fact, I am **still** in my night dress, Ascilla woke me up and.. w—we don't need to—talk more about that! The point is, you can tell. Kinda." Jomi clarified to Rhida as Mijo added, "You can tell from our voices too. Anyway," Mijo walks closer to Rhida, still a bit taller than Rhida. "What do you think? Repulsed?" asked Mijo, as Jomi is swarmed by Ikari and Lauvielle by questions. The others are talking to each other, and seeing as Mijo is busy with Rhida, they didn't want to disturb the **talk.** "A—ah?! I—I mean, I—I guess I prefer um... b—before—?!" Mijo moves closer to Rhida. "No, no.. I—I get it." Mijo nodded. "You want the fit, strong and *male* Mijo. It's fine. It's just for **this** party." Rhida is speechless before nodding. "I—I mean, I guess..?" Rhida looks at her own sparkly light blue dress. "Rhida, it's fine really. Just... treat me like you always do." assured Mijo, as Rhida nodded. "It's **weird**, it's the same woozy feelings with Ascilla... and, I—I.." Rhida hugs Mijo. "I—I want to know what it is. So, I—I'll accept you, in any form... okay?" Rhida smiled as she pulled back and looked at Mijo. "T—though, I—I mean that you look **human** at least.." clarified Rhida, shyly looking down. "Thank you.. and.." Mijo brushed her hair and added, "..yeah, it's harder if someone doesn't look at least human, I guess.." Rhida thinks, "Mmm... yeah. I don't know, does it feel bad to discriminate if.. sentient non-human beings *could* exist in the **dark world?**" Mijo looked at Rhida and said, "Um, I probably should talk to the others." Rhida nodded. "Yeah, I know.. this is a group party after all.." Rhida looked to JR. "Me and JR have been speculating on Manecony when I arrived. I'll.. get you the details that.. lead somewhere. Anyway, good bye, darling!" said Rhida, as Mijo nodded. "Mhm." Mijo turns to go to Urda, who joined in the Jomi circle. "Hey." Mijo says, as Jomi breathes a sigh of relief. "M—Mijo! Y—You're finally here.. they kept asking about potions, and.. Lady Ascilla! I was running out of breath.." said Jomi, exasperated. "Oh, right Mijo... um, how's.. how does being a woman feel like?" asked Lauvielle, as Mijo shrugged. "Normal. There's a difference in some areas.." Mijo looks down at her own body. "The thing is, it isn't really..." Mijo looks away. "..different for me." Mijo looks at Ikari. "I.. don't feel different." Ikari looks around before looking at Mijo. "Uh.. w—why..? I mean... yeah. I.. I can see that." replied Ikari before looking at Urda. "It feels like yourself, which is already you.." said Urda, pausing for a minute before continuing with, "..so it shouldn't. Things will probably change if someone's.. um.. self isn't known to others. Like, acquaintances, strangers.." Mijo nodded. "Isn't there at least a bit of surprise on my look?" "Buddy," Lauvielle tried to put her hand on Mijo's shoulder but she realized Mijo got taller due to her heels and so just casually held Mijo's arm. "We are in a world where we see people dressed up in their favourite anime character's clothes... Heck, it could even change if we want to be someone else." Lauvielle adds while looking up at Mijo. "So, you... trying out dresses? We get it. Though, I have an *important question.*" Lauvielle puts her hands up. "You said you could be referred to any *pronouns,* but.. we used he, since you... well, looked like one. I—If we were to.. speak of you after this meeting, what would you go by?" Mijo shrugged. "I'm..." Mijo looks at Urda, then Ikari before *she* looks at Lauvielle. "..not sure. But, like I said, **I don't care.** Though, if you **want** a rule, if you are referring to things I did as a man, refer as he. If I was a woman, like this party, use she." Mijo shrugs. "You can use they, but hey, that's what I want, if you want it simpler, my *main* is still he, but I don't recommend." "Huh, so... you're more.. ahem, *fluid* with your identity than I thought.." commented Ikari, as Mijo nodded. "Learnt that from **someone**." Mijo looks at Jomi. "Someone *she* has been meeting a lot." Jomi gasped in surprise mention and spoke up, "H—Hey! I'm just listening—w—who I meet in my time is.. secret..!" Jomi blushes faintly. "Anyways, this isn't *exactly* a... *permanent* affair..." said Mijo, as she steps back. "I just want to get a feel for it. That's all." Ikari shrugged. "Whatever you say.. um, bro?" Mijo waves his hand dismissively. "Yeah, yeah." Urda nodded. "Mhm, would your new body impeded your built *skills*? You know, videogame stuff, magic stuff.." Mijo shrugs as she goes and looks at the videogame console nearby, waiting to be turned on. "Let's see.." replied Mijo, before Jomi spoke up. "That! I actually just finished umm... making that. S—so, I'll be here if the system or.. hardware have problems." The four head there as Lauvielle asks, "How *advanced* is Kultima anyway? I know phones exist, robots definitely, but it feels more.. homely than my world that's like... *way* more advanced." Jomi explained, "We.. um.. we are about.. how do I explain this in light world terms... um, 1990s in terms of tech, but due to magic, combat is... well, I'd say it's fine for people using melees commonly." Jomi looks at Lauvielle. "You might think it's weird, but we don't have a use for *advanced weaponry* for abyssal monsters. And, it's not like it'll compete against **abyssal magic** users and tech." Jomi turns on the console. "And abyssal magic... well, it doesn't exactly need that. Though they could use it for.. more futuristic tech, I guess." Mijo and Urda sit down next to each other, Ikari and Lauvielle are separated by the two on the huge couch. Jomi is sat at the lone armchair next to the huge screen. "This.. this is nice." Mijo looks at Jamise and Leviente at a corner of the room, looking at Lauvielle then Mijo. The two look curious at Mijo, and amused at Lauvielle. Mijo looks back to the screen and sighs. Urda gives Mijo a controller. "Come on." she says before Mijo nods as the emulator program on screen loads a cooperative simulation game involving weird controls in moving items out of homes. "This... I.." Mijo smiled. ***"I'll enjoy it while it lasts."*** --- ## Author's Note: This took the better part of my vacation writing and life, though to be fair, it's easier to write fluff character exploration or world-building scenes than fight scenes.
